A: Optimum‚Äôs flexnode model distributes network roles dynamically across many independent participants instead of relying on fixed, centralized validators. yeah so the sequencer question is always a hot one since in most rollups it‚Äôs basically one party deciding transaction order, which is a centralization choke point. optimum‚Äôs trick is that ordering and propagation don‚Äôt depend on a single trusted machine. the rlnc layer turns data into coded packets, spreads them across many validators, and the deram memory layer keeps state consistent. so instead of one sequencer holding the pen, the network itself enforces order and availability. that way you get speed without turning it into a one-company show.
